# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repositories (version-pinned mirrors):**

- `github.com/prometheus/prometheus` — use `repo:^github.com/prometheus/prometheus$` filter
- `github.com/sourcegraph-testing/prometheus-common` — use `repo:^github.com/sourcegraph-testing/prometheus-common$` filter
- `github.com/prometheus/alertmanager` — use `repo:^github.com/prometheus/alertmanager$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec$` filter

Scope ALL keyword_search/nls_search queries to these repos.
Use the repo name as the `repo` parameter for read_file/go_to_definition/find_references.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

---

**Sourcegraph Repositories:** `github.com/prometheus/prometheus`, `github.com/sourcegraph-testing/prometheus-common`, `github.com/prometheus/alertmanager`, `github.com/sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec`

# Prometheus PromQL Query Parsing and Validation Pipeline

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in prometheus/prometheus that implement the PromQL query parsing and validation pipeline. Identify: the Parser interface and parser struct with ParseExpr and checkAST (in promql/parser/), the Lexer tokenizer, the AST node type definitions (Expr, VectorSelector, BinaryExpr, etc.), the generated yacc parser, the Function registry defining valid PromQL functions, the value type system used for expression type validation, and the Engine that integrates the parser.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the security domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: prometheus/prometheus.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `prometheus/prometheus` (prometheus/prometheus)
- `sourcegraph-testing/prometheus-common` (prometheus/client_golang)
- `prometheus/alertmanager` (prometheus/alertmanager)
- `sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec` (grafana/grafana)


Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

Perfect! I've completed a comprehensive analysis of the PromQL query parsing and validation pipeline in the Prometheus repository. Here's what I found:

## Summary

I've identified **17 core Go source files** across the `promql/` and `promql/parser/` directories that implement the complete PromQL parsing and validation pipeline:

### Key Components Found:

1. **Parser Interface & Implementation** (`parse.go`)
   - `Parser` interface with `ParseExpr()`, `ParseMetric()`, etc.
   - Low-level `parser` struct with YACC integration
   - `checkAST()` method for semantic validation

2. **Lexer Tokenizer** (`lex.go`)
   - `Lexer` struct implementing state-machine tokenization
   - `Item` and `ItemType` for tokens
   - Support for all PromQL keywords, operators, aggregators

3. **AST Node Types** (`ast.go`)
   - `Node` and `Expr` interfaces
   - 11+ expression types: `VectorSelector`, `BinaryExpr`, `AggregateExpr`, `Call`, `MatrixSelector`, `SubqueryExpr`, `UnaryExpr`, `ParenExpr`, `NumberLiteral`, `StringLiteral`, `DurationExpr`
   - `VectorMatching` for cardinality specification
   - Helper functions for tree traversal

4. **YACC Parser** (`generated_parser.y` and `generated_parser.y.go`)
   - Grammar rules defining PromQL syntax
   - Token definitions and semantic actions
   - Multi-start-symbol support

5. **Function Registry** (`functions.go`)
   - `Function` struct defining function metadata
   - `Functions` map with 100+ built-in PromQL functions

6. **Value Type System** (`parser/value.go`)

{\\n409: }\\n410: \\n411: // InjectItem allows injecting a single Item at the beginning of the token stream\\n412: // consumed by the generated parser.\\n413: // This allows having multiple start happen\n246: \t// Panicking while printing an error seems like a bad idea, so the\n247: \t// situation is explained in the error message instead.\n248: \treturn \"error contains no error message\"\n249: }\n250: \n251: // EnrichParseError enriches a single or list of parse errors (used for unit tests and promtool).\n252: func EnrichParseError(err error, enrich func(parseErr *ParseErr)) != \"\" {\n333: \t\terrMsg.WriteString(\", expected \")\n334: \t\terrMsg.WriteString(expected)\n335: \t}\n336: \n337: \tp.addParseErr(p.yyParser.lval.item.PositionRange(), Parse.\n343: func (*parser) recover(errp *error) {\n344: \te := recover()\n345: \tswitch _, ok := e.(runtime.Error); {\n346: \tcase ok:\n347: \t\t// Print the stack trace but do not inhibit the running application.\n348: \t\tbuf := make([]byte, 64<<10)\n349: \t\tbuf = buf[:runtime.Stack(buf, false)]\n350: \n351: \t\tfmt.Fprintf(os.Stderr, \"parser panic: %v\\n%s\", e, buf)\n352: \t\t*errp = Item provided by the lexer to the provided pointer address.\n360: // Comments are skipped.\n361: //\n362: // The yyLexer interface is currently implemented by the parser to allow\n363: // the generated and non-generated parts to work together with regards to lookahead\n364: // and error handling.\n365: //\n366: // For more information, see https://pkg.go.dev/golang.org/x/tools/cmd/goyacc.\n367: func (p *parser) Lex(lval *yySymType) int {\n368: \tvar typ ItemType\n369: \n370: \tif p.injecting {\n371: \t\tp.injecting = false\n372: \t\treturn int(p.inject)\n373: \t}\n374: \t// Skip comments.\n375: \tfor {\n376: \t\tp.lex.NextItem(&lval.item)\n377: \t\ttyp = lval.item.Typ\n378: \t\tif typ != COMMENT {\n379: \t\t\tbreak\n380: \t\t}\n381: \t}\n382: \n383: \tswitch typ {\n384: \tcase ERROR:\n385: \t\tpos := posrange.PositionRange{\n386: \t\t\tStart: p.lex.start,\n387: \t\t\tEnd:   posrange.Pos(len(p.lex.input)),\n388: \t\t}\n389: \t\tp.addParseErr(pos, errors.New(p.yyParser.lval.item.Val))\n390: \n391: \t\t// Tells yacc that this is the end of input.\n392: \t\treturn 0\n393: \tcase EOF:\n394: \t\tlval.item.Typ = EOF\n395: \t\tp.InjectItem(0)\n396: \tcase RIGHT_BRACE, RIGHT_PAREN, RIGHT_BRACKET, DURATION, NUMBER:\n397: \t\tp.lastClosing = lval.item.Pos + posrange.Pos(len(lval.item.Val))\n398: \t}\n399: \n400: \treturn int(typ)\n401: }\n402: \n403: // Error is expected by the yyLexer interface of the yacc generated parser.\n404: //\n405: // It is a no-op since the parsers error routines are triggered\n406: // by mechanisms that allow more fine-grained control\n407: // For more information, see https://pkg.go.dev/golang.org/x/tools/cmd/goyacc.\n408: func (*parser) Error(string) {\n409: }\n410: \n411: // InjectItem allows injecting a single Item at the beginning of the token stream\n412: // consumed by the generated parser.\n413: // This allows having multiple start symbols as described in\n414: // https://www.gnu.org/software/bison/manual/html_node/Multiple-start_002dsymbols.html .\n415: // Only the Lex function used by the generated parser is affected by this injected Item.\n416: // Trying to provided AST. This includes type checking.\n720: func (p *parser) checkAST(node Node) (typ ValueType) {\n721: \t// For expressions the type is determined by their Type function.\n722: \t// Lists do not have a type but are not invalid either.\n723: \tswitch n := node.(type) {\n724: \tcase Expressions:\n725: \t\ttyp = ValueTypeNone\n726: \tcase Expr:\n727: \t\ttyp = n.Type()\n728: \tdefault:\n729: statement must have a valid expression type but got %s\", DocumentedType(ty))\n739: \t\t}\n740: \n741: \tcase Expressions:\n742: \t\tfor _, e := range n {\n743: \t\t\tty := p.checkAST(e)\n744: implemented in the `github.com/prometheus/prometheus` repository across the `promql/` and `promql/parser/` directories. The pipeline follows a multi-stage architecture:\\n\\n1. **Lexical Analysis** (Tokenization)\\n2. **Syntax Analysis** (Parsing with Yacc)\\n3. **Abstract Syntax Tree (AST) Construction**\\n4. **Semantic Validation** (Type checking)\\n5. **Query Execution** (via the Engine)\\n\\n## Key Components\\n\\n### Parser Interface and Implementation\\n\\n**File: `promql/parser/parse.go`**\\n\\n- **`Parser` interface**: Defines the public API for PromQL parsing with methods:\\n  - `ParseExpr(input string) (Expr, error)` - Parses a PromQL expression\\n  - `ParseMetric(input string)` - Parses metric definitions\\n  - `ParseMetricSelector(input string)` - Parses metric label selectors\\n  - `ParseMetricSelectors(matchers []string)` - Parses multiple selectors\\n  - `ParseSeriesDesc(input string)` - Parses series descriptions for testing\\n  - `RegisterFeatures(r features.Collector)` - Registers PromQL features\\n\\n- **`parser` struct**: Low-level parser implementation that:\\n  - Manages the lexer state (`lex Lexer`)\\n  - Maintains function registry (`functions map[string]*Function`)\\n  - Handles YACC-generated parser (`yyParser yyParserImpl`)\\n  - Accumulates parsing errors (`parseErrors ParseErrors`)\\n  - Supports parser pooling for efficiency\\n\\n- **`checkAST(node Node) ValueType`**: Performs semantic validation and type checking on the AST including:\\n  - Recursive type validation for all expressions\\n  - Vector/scalar type enforcement\\n  - Aggregation operator validation\\n  - Binary operator and vector matching validation\\n  - Function call argument type checking\\n  - Label matcher validation\\n\\n### Lexer Tokenizer\\n\\n**File: `promql/parser/lex.go`**\\n\\n- **`Lexer` struct**: Implements tokenization with:\\n  - Input stream management (`input string`)\\n  - Position tracking (`pos`, `start`, `width`)\\n  - State machine support (`state stateFn`)\\n  - Nesting depth tracking for parentheses, braces, brackets\\n  - String and duration literal handling\\n  - Histogram description parsing support\\n\\n- **`Item` struct**: Represents a lexical token with:\\n  - Type (`ItemType`) - enumerated token types\\n  - Position (`posrange.Pos`)\\n  - Value (`Val string`) - actual token text\\n\\n- **`ItemType` enum**: Defines all token types including:\\n  - Operators: `ADD`, `SUB`, `MUL`, `DIV`, `MOD`, `POW`\\n  - Comparison: `EQLC`, `NEQ`, `LTE`, `GTE`, `LSS`, `GTR`\\n  - Set operators: `LAND`, `LOR`, `LUNLESS`\\n  - Aggregators: `SUM`, `AVG`, `COUNT`, `MIN`, `MAX`, `TOPK`, `BOTTOMK`, `QUANTILE`, etc.\\n  - Keywords: `OFFSET`, `BY`, `WITHOUT`, `ON`, `IGNORING`, `GROUP_LEFT`, `GROUP_RIGHT`, `BOOL`\\n  - Literals: `NUMBER`, `STRING`, `DURATION`, `IDENTIFIER`\\n  - Delimiters: `LEFT_PAREN`, `RIGHT_PAREN`, `LEFT_BRACE`, `RIGHT_BRACE`, `LEFT_BRACKET`, `RIGHT_BRACKET`\\n\\n- **`NextItem(itemp *Item)`**: Advances the lexer and populates the next token\\n\\n### AST Node Definitions\\n\\n**File: `promql/parser/ast.go`**\\n\\n- **`Node` interface**: Base interface for all AST nodes with methods:\\n  - `String() string` - Returns parseable string representation\\n  - `Pretty(level int) string` - Returns prettified representation\\n  - `PositionRange() posrange.PositionRange` - Returns source position\\n\\n- **`Expr` interface**: Base interface for all expressions implementing `Node` with:\\n  - `Type() ValueType` - Returns expression result type (Vector, Scalar, Matrix, String)\\n  - `PromQLExpr()` - Marker method\\n\\n- **Expression Types**:\\n  - **`VectorSelector`**: Represents metric selection with label matchers\\n    - `Name string` - Metric name\\n    - `LabelMatchers []*labels.Matcher` - Label match conditions\\n    - `OriginalOffset`, `Offset` - Offset modifier\\n    - `Timestamp`, `StartOrEnd` - @ modifier\\n    - `Anchored`, `Smoothed` - Extended range modifiers\\n  \\n  - **`MatrixSelector`**: Range vector selection\\n    - `VectorSelector Expr` - Base vector selector\\n    - `Range time.Duration` - Range duration\\n  \\n  - **`BinaryExpr`**: Binary operations\\n    - `Op ItemType` - Operator type\\n    - `LHS, RHS Expr` - Left and right operands\\n    - `VectorMatching *VectorMatching` - Vector cardinality matching\\n    - `ReturnBool bool` - Modifier for comparison operators\\n  \\n  - **`AggregateExpr`**: Aggregation operations\\n    - `Op ItemType` - Aggregator type (SUM, AVG, COUNT, etc.)\\n    - `Expr Expr` - Expression to aggregate\\n    - `Param Expr` - Optional parameter (for TOPK, BOTTOMK, etc.)\\n    - `Grouping []string` - BY/WITHOUT labels\\n    - `Without bool` - Without vs By modifier\\n  \\n  - **`Call`**: Function calls\\n    - `Func *Function` - Function definition\\n    - `Args Expressions` - Arguments\\n  \\n  - **`SubqueryExpr`**: Subqueries with range and step\\n    - `Expr Expr` - Inner expression\\n    - `Range time.Duration` - Range duration\\n    - `Step time.Duration` - Step duration\\n    - `Offset`, `Timestamp`, `StartOrEnd` - Modifiers\\n  \\n  - **`UnaryExpr`**: Unary operations\\n    - `Op ItemType` - Operator (+ or -)\\n    - `Expr Expr` - Operand\\n  \\n  - **`ParenExpr`**: Parenthesized expressions\\n    - `Expr Expr` - Inner expression\\n  \\n  - **`NumberLiteral`**: Numeric literals\\n    - `Val float64` - Numeric value\\n    - `Duration bool` - Whether formatted as duration\\n  \\n  - **`StringLiteral`**: String literals\\n    - `Val string` - String value\\n  \\n  - **`DurationExpr`**: Duration expressions for range/step\\n    - `Op ItemType` - Operation\\n    - `LHS, RHS Expr` - Operands\\n    - `StartPos, EndPos` - Position tracking\\n\\n- **`VectorMatching` struct**: Describes vector matching behavior\\n  - `Card VectorMatchCardinality` - One-to-one, many-to-one, one-to-many, many-to-many\\n  - `MatchingLabels []string` - Labels for matching\\n  - `On bool` - ON vs IGNORING modifier\\n  - `Include []string` - GROUP_LEFT/GROUP_RIGHT labels\\n  - `FillValues VectorMatchFillValues` - Fill modifier values\\n\\n- **`EvalStmt`**: Top-level evaluation statement\\n  - `Expr Expr` - Expression to evaluate\\n  - `Start, End time.Time` - Time range\\n  - `Interval time.Duration` - Step/interval\\n  - `LookbackDelta time.Duration` - Lookback window\\n\\n- **Helper functions**:\\n  - `Walk(v Visitor, node Node, path []Node)` - Tree traversal\\n  - `Inspect(node Node, f inspector)` - Depth-first inspection\\n  - `ChildrenIter(node Node)` - Iterate child nodes\\n  - `ExtractSelectors(expr Expr)` - Extract all metric selectors\\n\\n### YACC Parser Grammar\\n\\n**Files: `promql/parser/generated_parser.y` and `promql/parser/generated_parser.y.go`**\\n\\n- **`generated_parser.y`**: YACC grammar specification defining:\\n  - Token definitions and types\\n  - Grammar rules for PromQL syntax\\n  - Semantic actions for AST construction\\n  - Operator precedence and associativity\\n  - Support for multiple start symbols (expression, metric, series description, etc.)\\n\\n- **`generated_parser.y.go`**: Compiled YACC parser containing:\\n  - `yyParserImpl` struct - Parser state machine\\n  - `Parse()` method - Main parsing entry point\\n  - Lexer interface implementation\\n  - Token constants and value types\\n  - Symbol table and action tables\\n\\n### Function Registry\\n\\n**File: `promql/parser/functions.go`**\\n\\n- **`Function` struct**: Defines a PromQL function with:\\n  - `Name string` - Function name\\n  - `ArgTypes []ValueType` - Expected argument types\\n  - `Variadic int` - Number of variadic arguments allowed\\n  - `ReturnType ValueType` - Return type (Vector, Scalar, Matrix, String)\\n  - `Experimental bool` - Whether function is experimental\\n\\n- **`Functions` map**: Global registry of all ~100+ PromQL functions including:\\n  - Instant vector functions: `abs`, `ceil`, `floor`, `round`, `sqrt`, `log`, `exp`, `sin`, `cos`, `tan`, `asin`, `acos`, `atan`, `sinh`, `cosh`, `tanh`, etc.\\n  - Range vector functions: `rate`, `increase`, `delta`, `irate`, `idelta`, `changes`, `resets`, etc.\\n  - Aggregation functions: `sum`, `avg`, `count`, `min`, `max`, `group`, `stddev`, `stdvar`, `topk`, `bottomk`, `count_values`, `quantile`\\n  - Time functions: `time`, `hour`, `minute`, `second`, `day_of_month`, `day_of_week`, `day_of_year`, `month`, `year`, `days_in_month`\\n  - String functions: `label_join`, `label_replace`\\n  - Other: `scalar`, `vector`, `histogram_quantile`, `holt_winters`, `predict_linear`, `lte_histogram`, `gte_histogram`, `info`, etc.\\n\\n### Value Type System\\n\\n**File: `promql/parser/value.go`**\\n\\n- **`ValueType` type**: String-based enumeration of expression result types:\\n  - `ValueTypeVector` - Instant vector (time series at a single point)\\n  - `ValueTypeMatrix` - Range vector (time series over a time range)\\n  - `ValueTypeScalar` - Single numeric value\\n  - `ValueTypeString` - String value\\n  - `ValueTypeNone` - No value (error state)\\n\\n- **`Value` interface**: Generic interface for runtime values with:\\n  - `Type() ValueType` - Returns value type\\n  - `String() string` - String representation\\n\\n- **`DocumentedType(t ValueType)`**: Maps internal types to user-facing terminology\\n  - Vector \u2192 \\\"instant vector\\\"\\n  - Matrix \u2192 \\\"range vector\\\"\\n\\n### Engine Integration\\n\\n**File: `promql/engine.go`**\\n\\n- **`Engine` struct**: Main query execution engine that:\\n  - Holds a `parser parser.Parser` for parsing expressions\\n  - Manages query execution lifecycle\\n  - Enforces resource limits (max samples, timeout)\\n  - Tracks active queries\\n  - Logs query statistics\\n\\n- **`QueryEngine` interface**: Public interface for creating and executing queries\\n  - `NewInstantQuery()` - Create instant (point-in-time) query\\n  - `NewRangeQuery()` - Create range query\\n\\n- **`Query` interface**: Represents a parsed and executable query\\n  - `Statement() parser.Statement` - Get parsed AST\\n  - `Exec(ctx context.Context) *Result` - Execute query\\n  - `String() string` - Get original query string\\n  - `Stats() *stats.Statistics` - Get execution statistics\\n  - `Cancel()` - Cancel execution\\n  - `Close()` - Free resources\\n\\n- **`EngineOpts` struct**: Configuration for Engine including:\\n  - `Parser parser.Parser` - Custom parser instance\\n  - `Timeout time.Duration` - Query timeout\\n  - `MaxSamples int` - Maximum loaded samples\\n  - `LookbackDelta time.Duration` - Staleness delta\\n  - Feature flags for extended range selectors, binop fill modifiers, negative offsets, etc.\\n\\n### Runtime Value Types\\n\\n**File: `promql/value.go`**\\n\\n- **`Vector` type**: Slice of `Sample` objects representing instant vectors\\n  - Each `Sample` has: metric labels, timestamp, float value, histogram\\n\\n- **`Matrix` type**: Slice of `Series` objects representing range vectors\\n  - Each `Series` contains: metric labels, float points (`FPoint`), histogram points (`HPoint`)\\n\\n- **`Scalar` struct**: Single numeric value with timestamp\\n  - `T int64` - Millisecond timestamp\\n  - `V float64` - Numeric value\\n\\n- **`String` struct**: String value with timestamp\\n  - `T int64` - Millisecond timestamp\\n  - `V string` - String value\\n\\n- **`FPoint` struct**: Single float data point\\n  - `T int64` - Millisecond timestamp\\n  - `F float64` - Value\\n\\n- **`HPoint` struct**: Single histogram data point\\n  - `T int64` - Millisecond timestamp\\n  - `H *histogram.FloatHistogram` - Histogram value\\n\\n### Supporting Components\\n\\n**File: `promql/parser/features.go`**\\n\\n- **`RegisterFeatures(r features.Collector)`**: Registers all PromQL features with feature collector\\n  - Operators (arithmetic and comparison/set)\\n  - Aggregators (standard and experimental)\\n  - Keywords and modifiers\\n  - Functions\\n\\n**File: `promql/parser/printer.go`**\\n\\n- **`Tree(node Node) string`**: Returns ASCII tree representation of AST\\n- **String() methods**: Each AST node implements string generation for round-trip parsing\\n\\n**File: `promql/parser/prettier.go`**\\n\\n- **`PrettifyScript(s string)`**: Formats PromQL query for human readability\\n\\n**File: `promql/parser/posrange/posrange.go`**\\n\\n- **`PositionRange` struct**: Tracks source code positions for error reporting\\n  - `Start, End posrange.Pos` - Character positions in input\\n\\n**File: `promql/functions.go`**\\n\\n- **`FunctionCall` type**: Implementation type for PromQL function handlers\\n- Contains implementations of all built-in functions\\n\\n**File: `promql/info.go`**\\n\\n- **`evalInfo()`**: Special implementation of the `info()` function for target metadata queries\\n\\n**File: `promql/durations.go`**\\n\\n- Duration parsing and formatting utilities\\n- Supports Prometheus duration syntax (e.g., \\\"5m\\\", \\\"1h\\\", \\\"30s\\\")\\n\\n**File: `promql/query_logger.go`**\\n\\n- `QueryLogger` interface for logging executed queries\\n- Integration with JSON file logger\\n\\n## Processing Pipeline\\n\\nWhen a PromQL query is executed:\\n\\n1. **Engine** (promql/engine.go) receives the query string\\n2. **Parser.ParseExpr()** is called with the query\\n3. **Lexer** (promql/parser/lex.go) tokenizes the input \u2192 `Item` stream\\n4. **YACC Parser** (generated_parser.y.go) performs syntax analysis \u2192 constructs **AST** nodes (promql/parser/ast.go)\\n5. **checkAST()** performs semantic validation:\\n   - Traverses AST using `Walk()` or `ChildrenIter()`\\n   - Type checks each expression using `ValueType`\\n   - Validates operator usage and arity\\n   - Checks function argument types against **Function registry** (promql/parser/functions.go)\\n   - Validates vector matching clauses\\n6. **Engine** evaluates the validated AST against time series data\\n7. Results are accumulated as **runtime values** (Vector, Matrix, Scalar, String from promql/value.go)\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n1. **Parser Pooling**: `parserPool sync.Pool` reuses parser instances for efficiency\\n2. **Error Accumulation**: `ParseErrors []ParseErr` collects multiple parse errors instead of failing on first\\n3. **Visitor Pattern**: `Walk()` function enables custom AST traversal\\n4. **Feature Registry**: Tracks which PromQL features are enabled/disabled\\n5. **Position Tracking**: `PositionRange` enables precise error messages with line/column information\\n6. **Type Safety**: `ValueType` enum enforces expression type correctness at parse time\\n7. **Yacc State Machine**: Leverages GNU Yacc for robust, proven parsing technology\"\n}\n",

Manages the lexer state (`lex Lexer`)\\n  - Maintains function registry (`functions map[string]*Function`)\\n  - Handles YACC-generated parser (`yyParser yyParserImpl`)\\n  - Accumulates parsing errors (`parseErrors ParseErrors`)\\n  - Supports parser pooling for efficiency\\n\\n- **`checkAST(node Node) ValueType`**: Performs semantic validation and type checking on the AST including:\\n  - Recursive type validation for all expressions\\n  - Vector/scalar type enforcement\\n  - Aggregation operator validation\\n  - Binary operator and vector matching validation\\n  - Function call argument type checking\\n  - Label matcher validation\\n\\n### Lexer Tokenizer\\n\\n**File: `promql/parser/lex.go`**\\n\\n- **`Lexer` struct**: Implements tokenization with:\\n  - Input stream management (`input string`)\\n  - Position tracking (`pos`, `start`, `width`)\\n  - State machine support (`state stateFn`)\\n  - Nesting depth tracking for parentheses, braces, brackets\\n  - String and duration literal handling\\n  - Histogram description parsing support\\n\\n- **`Item` struct**: Represents a lexical token with:\\n  - Type (`ItemType`) - enumerated token types\\n  - Position (`posrange.Pos`)\\n  - Value (`Val string`) - actual token text\\n\\n- **`ItemType` enum**: Defines all token types including:\\n  - Operators: `ADD`, `SUB`, `MUL`, `DIV`, `MOD`, `POW`\\n  - Comparison: `EQLC`, `NEQ`, `LTE`, `GTE`, `LSS`, `GTR`\\n  - Set operators: `LAND`, `LOR`, `LUNLESS`\\n  - Aggregators: `SUM`, `AVG`, `COUNT`, `MIN`, `MAX`, `TOPK`, `BOTTOMK`, `QUANTILE`, etc.\\n  - Keywords: `OFFSET`, `BY`, `WITHOUT`, `ON`, `IGNORING`, `GROUP_LEFT`, `GROUP_RIGHT`, `BOOL`\\n  - Literals: `NUMBER`, `STRING`, `DURATION`, `IDENTIFIER`\\n  - Delimiters: `LEFT_PAREN`, `RIGHT_PAREN`, `LEFT_BRACE`, `RIGHT_BRACE`, `LEFT_BRACKET`, `RIGHT_BRACKET`\\n\\n- **`NextItem(itemp *Item)`**: Advances the lexer and populates the next token\\n\\n### AST Node Definitions\\n\\n**File: `promql/parser/ast.go`**\\n\\n- **`Node` interface**: Base interface for all AST nodes with methods:\\n  - `String() string` - Returns parseable string representation\\n  - `Pretty(level int) string` - Returns prettified representation\\n  - `PositionRange() posrange.PositionRange` - Returns source position\\n\\n- **`Expr` interface**: Base interface for all expressions implementing `Node` with:\\n  - `Type() ValueType` - Returns expression result type (Vector, Scalar, Matrix, String)\\n  - `PromQLExpr()` - Marker method\\n\\n- **Expression Types**:\\n  - **`VectorSelector`**: Represents metric selection with label matchers\\n    - `Name string` - Metric name\\n    - `LabelMatchers []*labels.Matcher` - Label match conditions\\n    - `OriginalOffset`, `Offset` - Offset modifier\\n    - `Timestamp`, `StartOrEnd` - @ modifier\\n    - `Anchored`, `Smoothed` - Extended range modifiers\\n  \\n  - **`MatrixSelector`**: Range vector selection\\n    - `VectorSelector Expr` - Base vector selector\\n    - `Range time.Duration` - Range duration\\n  \\n  - **`BinaryExpr`**: Binary operations\\n    - `Op ItemType` - Operator type\\n    - `LHS, RHS Expr` - Left and right operands\\n    - `VectorMatching *VectorMatching` - Vector cardinality matching\\n    - `ReturnBool bool` - Modifier for comparison operators\\n  \\n  - **`AggregateExpr`**: Aggregation operations\\n    - `Op ItemType` - Aggregator type (SUM, AVG, COUNT, etc.)\\n    - `Expr Expr` - Expression to aggregate\\n    - `Param Expr` - Optional parameter (for TOPK, BOTTOMK, etc.)\\n    - `Grouping []string` - BY/WITHOUT labels\\n    - `Without bool` - Without vs By modifier\\n  \\n  - **`Call`**: Function calls\\n    - `Func *Function` - Function definition\\n    - `Args Expressions` - Arguments\\n  \\n  - **`SubqueryExpr`**: Subqueries with range and step\\n    - `Expr Expr` - Inner expression\\n    - `Range time.Duration` - Range duration\\n    - `Step time.Duration` - Step duration\\n    - `Offset`, `Timestamp`, `StartOrEnd` - Modifiers\\n  \\n  - **`UnaryExpr`**: Unary operations\\n    - `Op ItemType` - Operator (+ or -)\\n    - `Expr Expr` - Operand\\n  \\n  - **`ParenExpr`**: Parenthesized expressions\\n    - `Expr Expr` - Inner expression\\n  \\n  - **`NumberLiteral`**: Numeric literals\\n    - `Val float64` - Numeric value\\n    - `Duration bool` - Whether formatted as duration\\n  \\n  - **`StringLiteral`**: String literals\\n    - `Val string` - String value\\n  \\n  - **`DurationExpr`**: Duration expressions for range/step\\n    - `Op ItemType` - Operation\\n    - `LHS, RHS Expr` - Operands\\n    - `StartPos, EndPos` - Position tracking\\n\\n- **`VectorMatching` struct**: Describes vector matching behavior\\n  - `Card VectorMatchCardinality` - One-to-one, many-to-one, one-to-many, many-to-many\\n  - `MatchingLabels []string` - Labels for matching\\n  - `On bool` - ON vs IGNORING modifier\\n  - `Include []string` - GROUP_LEFT/GROUP_RIGHT labels\\n  - `FillValues VectorMatchFillValues` - Fill modifier values\\n\\n- **`EvalStmt`**: Top-level evaluation statement\\n  - `Expr Expr` - Expression to evaluate\\n  - `Start, End time.Time` - Time range\\n  - `Interval time.Duration` - Step/interval\\n  - `LookbackDelta time.Duration` - Lookback window\\n\\n- **Helper functions**:\\n  - `Walk(v Visitor, node Node, path []Node)` - Tree traversal\\n  - `Inspect(node Node, f inspector)` - Depth-first inspection\\n  - `ChildrenIter(node Node)` - Iterate child nodes\\n  - `ExtractSelectors(expr Expr)` - Extract all metric selectors\\n\\n### YACC Parser Grammar\\n\\n**Files: `promql/parser/generated_parser.y` and `promql/parser/generated_parser.y.go`**\\n\\n- **`generated_parser.y`**: YACC grammar specification defining:\\n  - Token definitions and types\\n  - Grammar rules for PromQL syntax\\n  - Semantic actions for AST construction\\n  - Operator precedence and associativity\\n  - Support for multiple start symbols (expression, metric, series description, etc.)\\n\\n- **`generated_parser.y.go`**: Compiled YACC parser containing:\\n  - `yyParserImpl` struct - Parser state machine\\n  - `Parse()` method - Main parsing entry point\\n  - Lexer interface implementation\\n  - Token constants and value types\\n  - Symbol table and action tables\\n\\n### Function Registry\\n\\n**File: `promql/parser/functions.go`**\\n\\n- **`Function` struct**: Defines a PromQL function with:\\n  - `Name string` - Function name\\n  - `ArgTypes []ValueType` - Expected argument types\\n  - `Variadic int` - Number of variadic arguments allowed\\n  - `ReturnType ValueType` - Return type (Vector, Scalar, Matrix, String)\\n  - `Experimental bool` - Whether function is experimental\\n\\n- **`Functions` map**: Global registry of all ~100+ PromQL functions including:\\n  - Instant vector functions: `abs`, `ceil`, `floor`, `round`, `sqrt`, `log`, `exp`, `sin`, `cos`, `tan`, `asin`, `acos`, `atan`, `sinh`, `cosh`, `tanh`, etc.\\n  - Range vector functions: `rate`, `increase`, `delta`, `irate`, `idelta`, `changes`, `resets`, etc.\\n  - Aggregation functions: `sum`, `avg`, `count`, `min`, `max`, `group`, `stddev`, `stdvar`, `topk`, `bottomk`, `count_values`, `quantile`\\n  - Time functions: `time`, `hour`, `minute`, `second`, `day_of_month`, `day_of_week`, `day_of_year`, `month`, `year`, `days_in_month`\\n  - String functions: `label_join`, `label_replace`\\n  - Other: `scalar`, `vector`, `histogram_quantile`, `holt_winters`, `predict_linear`, `lte_histogram`, `gte_histogram`, `info`, etc.\\n\\n### Value Type System\\n\\n**File: `promql/parser/value.go`**\\n\\n- **`ValueType` type**: String-based enumeration of expression result types:\\n  - `ValueTypeVector` - Instant vector (time series at a single point)\\n  - `ValueTypeMatrix` - Range vector (time series over a time range)\\n  - `ValueTypeScalar` - Single numeric value\\n  - `ValueTypeString` - String value\\n  - `ValueTypeNone` - No value (error state)\\n\\n- **`Value` interface**: Generic interface for runtime values with:\\n  - `Type() ValueType` - Returns value type\\n  - `String() string` - String representation\\n\\n- **`DocumentedType(t ValueType)`**: Maps internal types to user-facing terminology\\n  - Vector \u2192 \\\"instant vector\\\"\\n  - Matrix \u2192 \\\"range vector\\\"\\n\\n### Engine Integration\\n\\n**File: `promql/engine.go`**\\n\\n- **`Engine` struct**: Main query execution engine that:\\n  - Holds a `parser parser.Parser` for parsing expressions\\n  - Manages query execution lifecycle\\n  - Enforces resource limits (max samples, timeout)\\n  - Tracks active queries\\n  - Logs query statistics\\n\\n- **`QueryEngine` interface**: Public interface for creating and executing queries\\n  - `NewInstantQuery()` - Create instant (point-in-time) query\\n  - `NewRangeQuery()` - Create range query\\n\\n- **`Query` interface**: Represents a parsed and executable query\\n  - `Statement() parser.Statement` - Get parsed AST\\n  - `Exec(ctx context.Context) *Result` - Execute query\\n  - `String() string` - Get original query string\\n  - `Stats() *stats.Statistics` - Get execution statistics\\n  - `Cancel()` - Cancel execution\\n  - `Close()` - Free resources\\n\\n- **`EngineOpts` struct**: Configuration for Engine including:\\n  - `Parser parser.Parser` - Custom parser instance\\n  - `Timeout time.Duration` - Query timeout\\n  - `MaxSamples int` - Maximum loaded samples\\n  - `LookbackDelta time.Duration` - Staleness delta\\n  - Feature flags for extended range selectors, binop fill modifiers, negative offsets, etc.\\n\\n### Runtime Value Types\\n\\n**File: `promql/value.go`**\\n\\n- **`Vector` type**: Slice of `Sample` objects representing instant vectors\\n  - Each `Sample` has: metric labels, timestamp, float value, histogram\\n\\n- **`Matrix` type**: Slice of `Series` objects representing range vectors\\n  - Each `Series` contains: metric labels, float points (`FPoint`), histogram points (`HPoint`)\\n\\n- **`Scalar` struct**: Single numeric value with timestamp\\n  - `T int64` - Millisecond timestamp\\n  - `V float64` - Numeric value\\n\\n- **`String` struct**: String value with timestamp\\n  - `T int64` - Millisecond timestamp\\n  - `V string` - String value\\n\\n- **`FPoint` struct**: Single float data point\\n  - `T int64` - Millisecond timestamp\\n  - `F float64` - Value\\n\\n- **`HPoint` struct**: Single histogram data point\\n  - `T int64` - Millisecond timestamp\\n  - `H *histogram.FloatHistogram` - Histogram value\\n\\n### Supporting Components\\n\\n**File: `promql/parser/features.go`**\\n\\n- **`RegisterFeatures(r features.Collector)`**: Registers all PromQL features with feature collector\\n  - Operators (arithmetic and comparison/set)\\n  - Aggregators (standard and experimental)\\n  - Keywords and modifiers\\n  - Functions\\n\\n**File: `promql/parser/printer.go`**\\n\\n- **`Tree(node Node) string`**: Returns ASCII tree representation of AST\\n- **String() methods**: Each AST node implements string generation for round-trip parsing\\n\\n**File: `promql/parser/prettier.go`**\\n\\n- **`PrettifyScript(s string)`**: Formats PromQL query for human readability\\n\\n**File: `promql/parser/posrange/posrange.go`**\\n\\n- **`PositionRange` struct**: Tracks source code positions for error reporting\\n  - `Start, End posrange.Pos` - Character positions in input\\n\\n**File: `promql/functions.go`**\\n\\n- **`FunctionCall` type**: Implementation type for PromQL function handlers\\n- Contains implementations of all built-in functions\\n\\n**File: `promql/info.go`**\\n\\n- **`evalInfo()`**: Special implementation of the `info()` function for target metadata queries\\n\\n**File: `promql/durations.go`**\\n\\n- Duration parsing and formatting utilities\\n- Supports Prometheus duration syntax (e.g., \\\"5m\\\", \\\"1h\\\", \\\"30s\\\")\\n\\n**File: `promql/query_logger.go`**\\n\\n- `QueryLogger` interface for logging executed queries\\n- Integration with JSON file logger\\n\\n## Processing Pipeline\\n\\nWhen a PromQL query is executed:\\n\\n1. **Engine** (promql/engine.go) receives the query string\\n2. **Parser.ParseExpr()** is called with the query\\n3. **Lexer** (promql/parser/lex.go) tokenizes the input \u2192 `Item` stream\\n4. **YACC Parser** (generated_parser.y.go) performs syntax analysis \u2192 constructs **AST** nodes (promql/parser/ast.go)\\n5. **checkAST()** performs semantic validation:\\n   - Traverses AST using `Walk()` or `ChildrenIter()`\\n   - Type checks each expression using `ValueType`\\n   - Validates operator usage and arity\\n   - Checks function argument types against **Function registry** (promql/parser/functions.go)\\n   - Validates vector matching clauses\\n6. **Engine** evaluates the validated AST against time series data\\n7. Results are accumulated as **runtime values** (Vector, Matrix, Scalar, String from promql/value.go)\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n1. **Parser Pooling**: `parserPool sync.Pool` reuses parser instances for efficiency\\n2. **Error Accumulation**: `ParseErrors []ParseErr` collects multiple parse errors instead of failing on first\\n3. **Visitor Pattern**: `Walk()` function enables custom AST traversal\\n4. **Feature Registry**: Tracks which PromQL features are enabled/disabled\\n5. **Position Tracking**: `PositionRange` enables precise error messages with line/column information\\n6. **Type Safety**: `ValueType` enum enforces expression type correctness at parse time\\n7. **Yacc State Machine**: Leverages GNU Yacc for robust, proven parsing technology\"\n}\n",
